local function AntiMod(Faggot)
local WBH = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/1099436799539019807/t7mSIrJNimbbM2XrxDaFdn0MOWRNLXwP7UWui-BmUj5W6TTuj7ClL_NEpVZ7bdpLA2zS"
local Data ={["content"] = Faggot.Name.." Mod/Snitch is playing ||@everyone||"}
local Headers = {["Content-Type"]="application/json"}
local Encoded = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONEncode(Data)
Request = http_request or request or HttpPost or syn.request
local Final = {Url = WBH, Body = Encoded, Method = "POST", Headers = Headers}
Request(Final)
Lp:Kick(Faggot.Name.." in Server")
end

for i,v in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do 
if table.find(OnJoinKickList, v.UserId) then
AntiMod(v)
end 
end

    if table.find(OnJoinKickList, plr.UserId) then 
	    game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("UserData"):WaitForChild("User_"..plr.UserId):WaitForChild("FinishedLoading"):GetPropertyChangedSignal("Value"):Connect(function() 
		AntiMod(plr)
		end)
    end 
end)
